</div>                            <div class="top10-section-list-text top10-content"><p>Credit card processing companies are at an advantage. They know that credit card processing is no longer optional for businesses, big or small. This has emboldened many to adopt some unsavory business practices.<strong> It’s not uncommon for a sales agent to sweet-talk a business into a great-sounding deal, only to laden them with exorbitant hidden fees</strong>.</p>
<p>Sadly, credit card processing companies are almost impossible to compare on the surface, as many offer no information on their site besides a few empty promises about how they are <i>definitely</i> your cheapest choice. These difficulties have caused many businesses to just accept a poor deal and service – but you don’t have to.</p>
<p><strong>We spent hundreds of hours putting together a list of the top 10 credit card processing companies operating today.</strong> To perform the most detailed comparison possible, we compiled thousands of merchant reviews, extensively compared features and pricing, and even tested the trustworthiness of each provider’s sales process ourselves.</p>
<p><strong>With our comparison, you’ll be able to minimize your processing fees while benefiting from some truly great features</strong>. Read through our findings below to find the right credit card processor for your business.</p>

<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">This makes Leaders Merchant Services a nice option if you’re already with a payment processor – </span><b>you can use your current rates as a starting point on the negotiation table</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">.</span></p>
<p><span style="font-weight: 400;">While merchants looking for their first payment processor won’t have </span><span style="font-weight: 400;">existing</span><span style="font-weight: 400;"> rates to beat, they’ll still </span><b>benefit from Leaders’ industry low </b><b>processing</b><b> rates</b><span style="font-weight: 400;">, quick approval, and impressive features such as customer loyalty programs, business loans, and cash advances.</span></p>

Its terminals integrate with a range of e-commerce software. </span></p>

                                    <div class="top10-vendor-list-item-content top10-content"><p>If you’re tired of credit card processors taking a sizable cut of every transaction, you’ll like Stax’s simple monthly payment model. You just pay a monthly subscription with no percentage-based markup. While there is a small flat fee per transaction in addition to the wholesale interchange rates, <strong>Stax’s per-transaction fees of </strong><strong><span class="pricing-link">0% + 10¢ (in-person)</span></strong><strong> are among the lowest in the industry. </strong></p>
<p>Due to the higher-than-usual monthly subscription, <strong>Stax’s pricing model makes sense If you’re processing over $8,000/month in card sales. </strong>High-volume businesses processing around $500,000 a year can <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=2631826&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_2631826_top10_1435_976567&post_id=1435&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="2631826" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_2631826_top10_1435_976567', 'stax', this,  true  );">save up to 40% with Stax</a> compared to a traditional processor that uses a percentage markup on every transaction.</p>
<p><strong>Stax is a particularly good option for online selling</strong>,  featuring a tool that allows you to create a custom shopping cart in a few clicks.                                     <div class="top10-vendor-list-item-content top10-content"><p>Starting an e-commerce business isn’t easy. Not only do you have to select a good payment processor, but you’ll also have to find a web hosting company that provides decent performance and store development tools. Helcim handles this for you by <strong>offering free web hosting, a store builder, and payment processing services.</strong></p>
<p>This is great if you’re selling online, but the picture isn’t quite as rosy if you take payments in a brick-and-mortar store. <strong>Helcim only integrates with a limited range of third-party POS hardware, which doesn’t include any third-party card terminals.</strong> Essentially, you’re forced to purchase its proprietary card reader outright.</p>
<p>Still, if you’re happy to use Helcim’s hardware, this all-in-one solution definitely makes things easier. <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=2645295&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_2645295_top10_1435_981185&post_id=1435&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&positioninlist=1&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="2645295" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_2645295_top10_1435_981185', 'helcim', this,  true  );">Helcim’s platform is super user-friendly</a> – every aspect, from store and checkout creation to customer &amp; inventory management, requires zero code and can be controlled with a few clicks. Best of all, <strong>Helcim doesn’t lock you into a contract</strong> – you can cancel anytime without paying a fee.</p>

                                    <div class="top10-vendor-list-item-content top10-content"><p><strong>POS Pros’ <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=2950747&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_2950747_top10_1435_895019&post_id=1435&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&positioninlist=1&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="2950747" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_2950747_top10_1435_895019', 'pos-pros', this,  true  );">industry-specific approach to POS solutions</a></strong><strong> offers a lot to businesses that rely mostly on in-person transactions</strong>. Restaurants, retailers, hotels, and healthcare practitioners can all benefit from this approach, which takes into account not just your business type, but also its size and unique processing needs.</p>
<p>During an initial consultation, a POS Pros specialist will recommend several point-of-sale equipment options. <strong>You’ll then be able to test the interface and features of each POS system during a free virtual demo. </strong>This personalized approach can help both new and established businesses avoid buying the wrong equipment.</p>
<p>While POS Pros offers interchange plus, tiered pricing, and cash discount plans for both brick-and-mortar and e-commerce merchants, it doesn’t post pricing and fees on its website. While this quote-only approach has its advantages, it can make it more difficult if you’re comparing multiple processors to determine which is your best option.</p>

                                    <div class="top10-vendor-list-item-content top10-content"><p>If you operate in a high-risk industry or have a poor credit score, you’ll probably find that many credit card processors won’t even speak to you. Thankfully, <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=2631829&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_2631829_top10_1435_986549&post_id=1435&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="2631829" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_2631829_top10_1435_986549', 'paymentcloud', this,  true  );"><strong>PaymentCloud has a 98% approval rate</strong></a><strong> </strong><strong>– one of the highest in the US.</strong></p>
<p>While mid and high-risk merchants are charged a slightly higher percentage markup per transaction, the rates are reasonable compared to other high-risk payment processors that often take advantage of your narrower range of choice.</p>
<p>In addition to providing a free POS terminal, PaymentCloud can set up a virtual terminal and payment gateway for you. Furthermore, <strong>PaymentCloud has one of the longest lists of accepted payment methods I’ve seen from a credit card processor</strong>. It even accepts crypto, including popular coins such as Bitcoin, Ethereum, and Monero.</p>

<h2 id="hselect-2">How Do We Evaluate Credit Card Processors?</h2>
<p></p> Unlike other review sites, <strong>we at Website Planet believe you deserve to know more than just the surface-level details of each credit card processor</strong>. To get at the truth beyond the marketing, here are the measures we take to evaluate the payment processors we review. 
<h3>Features</h3>
<p></p> Obviously you need your credit card processor to process payments, but this isn’t all a good processor should offer. <strong>The best credit card processors also make running your business and managing your finances far easier</strong> by giving you management tools, detailed analytics, and integratable e-commerce and POS solutions. 
<p></p> We separately research the features listed by every payment processor to get at the reality behind all the marketing jargon. This allows us to determine what, if anything, really stands. For example, <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=2631449&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_2631449_top10_1435_895020&post_id=1435&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&positioninlist=1&amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="2631449" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_2631449_top10_1435_895020', 'leaders-merchant-services', this,  true  );"><b>Leaders Merchant Services’ e-commerce tools</b></a><b> and integrations are</b><strong> among the most versatile in the business </strong>– even more so than those offered by more expensive payment processors. 
<h3>Ease of Use</h3>
<p></p> <strong>Most businesses simply want something that works, and works well</strong>. No one wants to get trapped in hours of setup and coding just to get their payment processor to integrate with their backend. After all, time is valuable – the best credit card processors can be set up in minutes. 
<p></p> That’s why we evaluate every payment processor on its overall ease of use. Will a beginner have difficulty setting things up? Are there guides or training available? How user-friendly is the platform? These are just some of the questions we ask when considering how easy to use a platform really is. 
<h3>Compliance and Security</h3>
<p></p> Security is a priority. <strong>If your payment processor cannot ensure PCI-compliance, your business could face heavy fines and class-action lawsuits</strong>. A data breach can easily bring an otherwise successful business to its knees, and customers need to be able to trust you if they&#8217;re going to hand over their money and data. 
<p></p> <strong>That’s why we ensure that every credit card processor we review is PCI-compliant</strong>. We also check overall security standards, whether data breaches occurred in the past, and more. Additional protections against fraud and chargebacks are always a bonus. 
<h3>Pricing</h3>
<p></p> <strong>Credit card processors have a reputation for smuggling non-disclosed fees into their contracts</strong>. To make matters worse, many payment processors completely hide their rates, forcing you to ring their sales line. This immediately puts you at a disadvantage, as the trained sales agent has all the information while you have none. 
<p></p> We cut through this obscurity to give you more precise details on what you can expect to pay. That way, you can make an informed decision. We also reward credit card processors who offer transparent pricing information, which is something we’d love to see become the norm. 
<h3>Support</h3>
<p></p> If the finances of your business are at stake, there had better be a responsive support team to help whenever there’s an issue. You can find plenty of horror stories online where crucial funds were withheld from merchants and the credit card processor&#8217;s support team just didn’t seem to care. 
<p></p> <strong>Testing the support team of each credit card processor is an important part of all our reviews. </strong>We call the sales team ourselves to find out whether they give honest and helpful information, and we also evaluate the responsiveness and availability of the technical support team. 
<h2 id="hselect-3">FAQ</h2>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Which credit card processor is best?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">This depends on many factors, such as your industry, transaction volume, average transaction amount, and more. <span style="font-weight: 400;">That said,</span><b> <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=2631449&#038;lang=en&#038;deep_id=0&#038;deep_name=&#038;btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_2631449_top10_1435_894917&#038;post_id=1435&#038;pageview_id=0&#038;direct_link=&#038;type=top10&#038;positioninlist=1&#038;amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="2631449" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_2631449_top10_1435_894917', 'leaders-merchant-services', this,  true  );">Leaders Merchant Services is an excellent choice</a></b><span style="font-weight: 400;"> for most businesses, offering reliable low-cost interchange plus processing, innovative POS solutions, and a meet-or-beat guarantee.</span> 
<p></p> Otherwise, you can check out our comparison of the <a href="#leaders-merchant-services" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'leadersmerchantservices', this,  );">top 10 credit card processors above</a> to get a feel for which processor might be a good fit for your business. For more information on a particular one, be sure to check out its detailed review.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What is the largest credit card processor in the US?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">The largest payment processors in the US tend to be banks, such as Bank of America and First Data. However, this doesn’t mean that they are good options. They tend to charge high processing fees and offer little to no features that can help manage your business and finances. All of <a href="#leaders-merchant-services" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'leadersmerchantservices', this,  );">the credit card processors above</a> offer better value.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What are typical credit card processing fees?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Most businesses will pay 1.5% – 4.5% of every cashless transaction in processing fees. The exact percentage will vary depending on the interchange rate charged by card-issuing banks, as well as the pricing model and fees charged by the credit card processor. For example, Leaders Merchant Services <a href="#leaders-merchant-services" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'leadersmerchantservices', this,  );">(LMS) is among the cheapest interchange processors</a>, charging only <span class="pricing-link"><span data-currency="USD" class="currency-symbol ">$</span><span data-currency="USD" data-price="9.00" class="currency-value">9.00</span></span>/month and <span class="pricing-link">~2% + 0¢</span>/transaction, on average. On the other hand, <a href="#stax" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'stax', this,  );">Stax, with its subscription pricing model</a>, charges a higher monthly fee starting at <span class="pricing-link"><span data-currency="USD" class="currency-symbol ">$</span><span data-currency="USD" data-price="99.00" class="currency-value">99.00</span></span> in exchange for low transaction fees of <span class="pricing-link">0% + 10¢ (in-person)</span>.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What is the fastest credit card processor?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline"><a href="#square-payments" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'squarepayments', this,  );">Square offers instant access to your funds</a> through its small business checking account. <a href="#chase-payment-solutions" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickin', 'anchorLink', 'chasepaymentsolutions', this,  );">Another option for fast payouts is Chase</a> Payment Solutions, which offers same-day payouts for Chase banking customers and next-day payouts for all other merchants.</span> 
</div>
